---
This topic lists file formats supported by GroupDocs.Conversion for .NET.


## Image formats

| Format | Description | Load | Save | Automatic format detection |
| --- | --- | :---: | :---: | :---: |
| [AI](https://docs.fileformat.com/image/ai/) | Adobe Illustrator Artwork |<!--Load--> ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |<!--Save-->  |<!--Auto-detect--> ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |

## eBook formats

| Format | Description | Load | Save | Automatic format detection |
| --- | --- | :---: | :---: | :---: |
| [EPUB](https://docs.fileformat.com/ebook/epub/) | Open eBook Format |<!--Load--> ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |<!--Save-->  ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |<!--Auto-detect--> ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |
| [MOBI](https://docs.fileformat.com/ebook/mobi/) |  Mobipocket eBook |<!--Load--> ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |<!--Save-->  |<!--Auto-detect--> ![(tick)](/conversion/net/images/check-blue.png) |

Refer to the following help topic for details on how to use GroupDocs.Conversion to eBook files: [Convert eBook](/conversion/net/convert/ebook2/).
